|| die "ERROR: JAVA_HOME is not set and no 'java' command could be found in your PATH.<\n><\n>Please set the JAVA_HOME variable in your environment to match the<\n>location of your Java installation."<\n>fi<\n><\n># Escape application args<\n>save () {<\n>    for i do printf %s\\n "$i" | sed "s/'/'\\\\''/g;1s/^/'/;\$s/\$/' \\\\/" ; done<\n>    echo " "<\n>}<\n>APP_ARGS=$(save   modImplementation "net.fabricmc.fabric-api:fabric-api:${project.fabric_version}"<\n>    <\n>    implementation 'com.google.code.gson:gson:2.10.1'<\n>}<\n><\n>processResources {<\n> {<\n>    from("LICENSE") {<\n>        rename { "${it}_${project.archivesBaseName}"}<\n>    }<\n>}<\n>EOF<\n><\n>echo " Creating Java source files..."<\n><\n># Create NameHistoryMod.java<\n>cat > src/main/java/com/liforra/namehistory/NameHistoryMod.java << 'EOF'<\n>package com.liforra.namehistory;<\n><\n>import com.liforra.namehistory.api.ApiConfig;<\n>import com.liforra.namehistory.command.NameHistoryCommand;<\n>import net.fabricmc.api.ClientModInitializer;<\n>import net.fabricmc.fabric.api.client.command.v2.ClientCommandRegistrationCallback;<\n>import org.slf4j.Logger;<\n>import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;<\n><\n>public class NameHistoryMod implements ClientModInitializer {<\n>    public static final String MOD_ID = "namehistory";<\n>    public static ApiConfig.load();<\n>        <\n>        ClientCommandRegistrationCallback.EVENT.register((dispatcher, registryAccess) -> {<\n>            NameHistoryCommand.register(dispatcher);<\n>        });<\n>        <\n>        LOGGER.info("NameHistory Mod initialized");<\n>    }<\n>}<\n>EOF<\n><\n># Create NameHistoryCommand.java<\n>cat > src/main/java/com/liforra/namehistory/command/NameHistoryCommand.java << 'EOF'<\n>package com.liforra.namehistory.command;<\n><\n>import com.liforra.namehistory.api.ApiClient;<\n>import com.liforra.namehistory.api.ApiConfig;<\n>import com.liforra.namehistory.api.model.*;<\n>import com.liforra.namehistory.util.TextFormatter;<\n>import com.mojang.brigadier.CommandDispatcher;<\n>import com.mojang.brigadier.arguments.StringArgumentType;<\n>import com.mojang.brigadier.context.CommandContext;<\n>import net.fabricmc.fabric.api.client.command.v2.FabricClientCommandSource;<\n>import net.minecraft.text.Text;<\n><\n>import java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture;<\n><\n>import static net.fabricmc.fabric.api.client.command.v2.ClientCommandManager.*;<\n><\n>public class NameHistoryCommand {<\n>    private static final ApiClient apiClient = new ApiClient();<\n><\n>    public static void register(CommandDispatcher<FabricClientCommandSource> dispatcher) {<\n>        dispatcher.register(literal("namehistory")<\n>            .then(literal("get")<\n>                .then(argument("username", StringArgumentType.string())<\n>                    .executes(ctx -> getByUsername(ctx, StringArgumentType.getString(ctx, "username")))))<\n>            <\n>            .then(literal("uuid")<\n>                .then(argument("uuid", StringArgumentType.string())<\n>                    .executes(ctx -> getByUuid(ctx, StringArgumentType.getString(ctx, "uuid")))))<\n>            <\n>            .then(literal("update")<\n>                .then(argument("username", StringArgumentType.string())<\n>                    .executes(ctx -> updateProfile(ctx, StringArgumentType.getString(ctx, "username")))))<\n>            <\n>            .then(literal("delete")<\n>                .then(argument("username", StringArgumentType.string())<\n>                    .executes(ctx -> deleteProfile(ctx, StringArgumentType.getString(ctx, "username")))))<\n>            <\n>            .then(literal("config")<\n>                .then(literal("set")<\n>                    .then(argument("url", StringArgumentType.greedyString())<\n>                        .executes(ctx -> setApiUrl(ctx, StringArgumentType.getString(ctx, "url")))))<\n>                .then(literal("get")<\n>                    .executes(NameHistoryCommand::getApiUrl)))<\n>            <\n>            .executes(NameHistoryCommand::showHelp)<\n>        );<\n>    }<\n><\n>    private static int showHelp(CommandContext<FabricClientCommandSource> ctx) {<\n>        ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(Text.literal("6=== NameHistory Commands ==="));<\n>        ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(Text.literal("e/namehistory get <username> 7- Get name history"));<\n>        ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(Text.literal("e/namehistory uuid <uuid> 7- Get by UUID"));<\n>        ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(Text.literal("e/namehistory update <username> 7- Force update"));<\n>        ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(Text.literal("e/namehistory delete <username> 7- Delete from cache"));<\n>        ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(Text.literal("e/namehistory config set <url> 7- Set API URL"));<\n>        ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(Text.literal("e/namehistory config get 7- Show current API URL"));<\n>        return 1;<\n>    }<\n><\n>    private static int getByUsername(CommandContext<FabricClientCommandSource> ctx, String username) {<\n>        ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(Text.literal("7Fetching history for e" + username + "7..."));<\n>        <\n>        CompletableFuture.runAsync(() -> {<\n>            try {<\n>                ProfileHistory history = apiClient.getNameHistory(username);<\n>                ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(TextFormatter.formatProfileHistory(history));<\n>            } catch (Exception e) {<\n>                ctx.getSource().sendError(Text.literal("cError: " + e.getMessage()));<\n>            }<\n>        });<\n>        <\n>        return 1;<\n>    }<\n><\n>    private static int getByUuid(CommandContext<FabricClientCommandSource> ctx, String uuid) {<\n>        ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(Text.literal("7Fetching history for UUID e" + uuid + "7..."));<\n>        <\n>        CompletableFuture.runAsync(() -> {<\n>            try {<\n>                ProfileHistory history = apiClient.getNameHistoryByUuid(uuid);<\n>                ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(TextFormatter.formatProfileHistory(history));<\n>            } catch (Exception e) {<\n>                ctx.getSource().sendError(Text.literal("cError: " + e.getMessage()));<\n>            }<\n>        });<\n>        <\n>        return 1;<\n>    }<\n><\n>    private static int updateProfile(CommandContext<FabricClientCommandSource> ctx, String username) {<\n>        ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(Text.literal("7Updating profile for e" + username + "7..."));<\n>        <\n>        CompletableFuture.runAsync(() -> {<\n>            try {<\n>                UpdateRequest request = new UpdateRequest();<\n>                request.username = username;<\n>                <\n>                UpdateResponse response = apiClient.updateProfiles(request);<\n>                <\n>                if (!response.updated.isEmpty()) {<\n>                    ProfileHistory history = response.updated.get(0);<\n>                    ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(Text.literal("aProfile updated successfully!"));<\n>                    ctx.getSource().sendFeedback(TextFormatter.formatProfileHistory(history));<\n>                } else if (!response.errors.isEmpty()) {<\n>                    UpdateResponse.ErrorEntry error = response.errors.get(0);<\n>                    ctx.getSource().sendError(Text.literal("cUpdate failed: " + error.error));<\n>                }<\n>            } catch (Exception e) {<\n> #!/bin/bash<\n><\n># Output file<\n>OUT_FILE="packages_to_delete.txt"<\n><\n># Check for fzf<\n>if ! command -v fzf &> /dev/null; then<\n>    echo "Error: 'fzf' is not installed."<\n>    echo "Please run: sudo pacman -S fzf"<\n>    exit 1<\n>fi<\n><\n>echo "Generating package list (this takes a second)..."<\n><\n># 1. Get Explicitly Installed (-Qe) packages with info (-i)<\n># 2. Parse with awk to get: Size Unit Name Description<\n># 3. Sort by human readable size (-hr)<\n># 4. Column makes it pretty aligned<\n>LC_ALL=C pacman -Qei | \<\n>awk '/^Name/{name=$3} /^Desc/{d=""; for(i=3;i<=NF;i++) d=d" "$i} /^Installed Size/{print $4$5, name, d}' | \<\n>sort -hr | \<\n>column -t -s ' ' | \<\n>fzf --multi \<\n>    --layout=reverse \<\n>    --border \<\n>    --margin=1,2 \<\n>    --header="[TAB] Select/Deselect | [ENTER] Confirm | [ESC] Cancel" \<\n>    --prompt="Search Packages > " \<\n>    --preview='pacman -Qi {2}' \<\n>    --preview-window='right:50%:wrap' \<\n>    | awk '{print $2}' > "$OUT_FILE"<\n><\n># Check if file has content<\n>if [ -s "$OUT_FILE" ]; then<\n>    COUNT=$(wc -l < "$OUT_FILE")<\n>    echo ""<\n>    echo "---------------------------------------------------"<\n>    echo " Success! $COUNT packages saved to '$OUT_FILE'"<\n>    echo "---------------------------------------------------"<\n>    echo "To delete them, run:"<\n>    echo "sudo pacman -Rns - < $OUT_FILE"<\n>else<\n>    echo "No packages selected."<\n>    rm -f "$OUT_FILE"<\n>fi

#!/usr/bin/env bash<\n>set -euo pipefail<\n><\n>INPUT_FILE="ytdlp.txt"<\n>OUT_DIR="./downloaded-vids"<\n><\n>mkdir -p "$OUT_DIR"<\n><\n>if [[ ! -f "$INPUT_FILE" ]]; then<\n>  echo "Input file not found: $INPUT_FILE" >&2<\n>  exit 1<\n>fi<\n><\n># Video preference: 1080p, then 720p, then best <=1080p<\n>VIDEO_PREF="bestvideo[height=1080]/bestvideo[height=720]/bestvideo[height<=1080]/bestvideo"<\n><\n># Audio preference: avoid auto-dub/descriptive tracks<\n># Using single quotes to prevent bash interpretation of special characters<\n>AUDIO_PREF='bestaudio[vcodec=none][role!=dub][role!=descriptive][role!=commentary]/bestaudio[vcodec=none][role!=dub]/bestaudio[vcodec=none]'<\n><\n>FORMAT="(${VIDEO_PREF})+(${AUDIO_PREF})/best"<\n><\n># Graceful Ctrl-C handling<\n>trap 'echo; echo "Interrupted"; exit 130' INT<\n><\n># Read non-empty, non-comment lines<\n>while IFS= read -r url; do<\n>  [[ -z "$url" || "$url" =~ ^[[:space:]]*# ]] && continue<\n><\n>  echo "Downloading: $url"<\n>  yt-dlp \<\n>    -f "$FORMAT" \<\n>    -S "res:1080,codec:h264,br,acodec" \<\n>    --merge-output-format mp4 \<\n>    --no-part \<\n>    --restrict-filenames \<\n>    -o "$OUT_DIR/%(title)s-%(id)s.%(ext)s" \<\n>    "$url" || {<\n>      echo "Failed: $url" >&2<\n>    }<\n>done < "$INPUT_FILE"<\n><\n>echo "All done. Files in: $OUT_DIR"

exec -a bash /bin/sh -c '<\n>if [ -n "$BASH_VERSION" ]; then<\n>    echo "/bin/sh is bash"<\n>elif (echo "echo \$BASH_VERSION" | /bin/sh) 2>/dev/null | grep -q .; then<\n>    echo "/bin/sh is bash (non-login)"<\n>elif (echo "echo {1..2}" | /bin/sh) >/dev/null 2>&1; then<\n>    echo "/bin/sh is zsh (brace expansion)"<\n>elif (echo "typeset foo=bar" | /bin/sh) >/dev/null 2>&1; then<\n>    echo "/bin/sh is ksh"<\n>elif (echo "echo \$((1+1))" | /bin/sh) >/dev/null 2>&1; then<\n>    echo "/bin/sh is dash or ash (POSIX only)"<\n>else<\n>    echo "/bin/sh is unknown"<\n>fi<\n>'<\n>
